FIX_SESSION_ID = \"CamelFixSessionID\";\n\n    @Metadata(description = \"The FIX sender CompID\")\n    public static final String FIX_SENDER_COMP_ID = \"CamelFixSenderCompID\";\n\n    @Metadata(description = \"The FIX target CompID\")\n    public static final String FIX_TARGET_COMP_ID = \"CamelFixTargetCompID\";\n}\n```\n\n### File: components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixConsumer.java\n```java\npublic class FixConsumer extends DefaultConsumer implements FixMessageListener {\n    private final FixEndpoint endpoint;\n\n    @Override\n    protected void doStart() throws Exception {\n        super.doStart();\n        // Register with FIX engine\n        FixComponent component = endpoint.getComponent();\n        if (component != null && component.getFixEngine() != null) {\n            component.getFixEngine().addMessageListener(endpoint.getSessionID(), this);\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onMessage(String message) {\n        try {\n            // Create exchange for incoming FIX message\n            Exchange exchange = createExchange();\n            exchange.getIn().setBody(message);\n            exchange.getIn().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_SESSION_ID, endpoint.getSessionID());\n\n            // Process through Camel route\n            getProcessor().process(exchange);\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            LOG.error(\"Error processing FIX message\", e);\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### File: components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixProducer.java\n```java\npublic class FixProducer extends DefaultAsyncProducer {\n    private final FixEndpoint endpoint;\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean process(Exchange exchange, AsyncCallback callback) {\n        try {\n            String message = exchange.getIn().getBody(String.class);\n            if (message == null) {\n                exchange.setException(new IllegalArgumentException(\"FIX message body cannot be null\"));\n                callback.done(false);\n                return false;\n            }\n\n            // Send via FIX engine\n            FixComponent component = endpoint.getComponent();\n            if (component != null && component.getFixEngine() != null) {\n                component.getFixEngine().sendMessage(endpoint.getSessionID(), message);\n            } else {\n                exchange.setException(new IllegalStateException(\"FIX engine is not available\"));\n                callback.done(false);\n                return false;\n            }\n\n            callback.done(true);\n            return true;\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            LOG.error(\"Error sending FIX message\", e);\n            exchange.setException(e);\n            callback.done(false);\n            return false;\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### File: FixMessageListener listener);\n}\n```\n\n### File: components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixMessageListener.java\n```java\npublic interface FixMessageListener {\n    void components/camel-fix/src/main/resources/META-INF/services/org/apache/camel/component/fix\n```\nclass=org.apache.camel.component.fix.FixComponent\n```\n\n## Implementation Strategy\n\n### Architecture Overview\nThe FIX component follows Apache Camel's standard component architecture:\n\n1. **Component Lifecycle**: FixComponent manages the global FIX engine instance and creates endpoints per session ID\n2. **Endpoint Model**: FixEndpoint represents a connection to a specific FIX session and produces/consumes messages\n3. **Async Processing**: FixProducer uses DefaultAsyncProducer with AsyncCallback for non-blocking sends\n4. **Message Routing**: FixConsumer implements FixMessageListener to receive messages from the engine and feed them into Camel routes\n5. **Configuration**: FixConfiguration uses @UriParams for injectable URI options (configFile, senderCompID, targetCompID, etc.)\n\n### Key Design Decisions\n\n1. **Engine Abstraction**: FixEngine interface allows pluggable FIX protocol implementations (QuickFIX/J, custom implementations)\n2. **Listener Pattern**: FixMessageListener provides a clean callback mechanism for the FIX engine to notify the consumer of incoming messages\n3. **Session-based Routing**: sessionID in URI syntax (fix:sessionID?options) enables multiple concurrent FIX sessions\n4. **Async Producer**: DefaultAsyncProducer allows non-blocking message sends to fit Camel's async model\n5. **Configuration Inheritance**: Component-level configuration is copied to endpoints with option parameter overrides\n6. **Metadata Annotation**: @Metadata annotations enable documentation generation and component discovery\n\n### Integration Points\n\n- **Component Discovery**: META-INF/services file enables Camel's service loader to discover the FixComponent\n- **URI Endpoint**: @UriEndpoint annotation registers the scheme and syntax with Camel's URI parser\n- **Header Constants**: FixConstants enables type-safe access to FIX-specific message headers\n- **Parent POM**: Inherits from components parent for consistent build configuration\n- **Module Registration**: Added to components/pom.xml for multi-module Maven build\n\n## Files Created\n\n- `/workspace/components/camel-fix/pom.xml` — Maven module definition\n- `/workspace/components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixComponent.java` — Annotation: `@org.apache.camel.spi.annotations.Component(\"name\")`\n   - Method: `protected Endpoint createEndpoint(String uri, String remaining, Map<String, Object> parameters)`\n   - Manages: component-level lifecycle, shared resources, configuration defaults\n\n2. **Endpoint** (extends DefaultEndpoint)\n   - Annotation: `@UriEndpoint(scheme=\"fix\", syntax=\"fix:sessionID\", category={...}, headersClass=...)`\n   - Methods: `createProducer()`, `createConsumer(Processor)`\n   - Manages: session-specific configuration, endpoint lifecycle\n\n3. **Configuration** (POJO)\n   - Annotation: `@UriParams` on class\n   - Annotation: `@UriParam` on fields for injectable URI parameters\n   - Annotation: `@Metadata` on fields for documentation\n   - Pattern: Copy from component to endpoint in createEndpoint()\n\n4. **Producer** (extends DefaultAsyncProducer for async, or DefaultProducer)\n   - Async: implements `boolean process(Exchange exchange, AsyncCallback callback)`\n   - Sync: implements `void process(Exchange exchange)`\n   - Must call `callback.done(true/false)` for async\n\n5. **Consumer** (extends DefaultConsumer)\n   - Methods: `doStart()`, `doStop()` for lifecycle\n   - Pattern: Register listener in doStart(), unregister in doStop()\n   - Uses: `getProcessor().process(exchange)` to feed messages into route\n\n6. **Constants** (utility class)\n   - Annotation: `@Metadata` on each constant for documentation\n   - Purpose: Type-safe header keys and other magic strings\n\n### URI Pattern\n- Format: `scheme:path?option1=value1&option2=value2`\n- Example: `fix:SESSION1?configFile=/etc/fix.cfg&senderCompID=TRADER`\n- Path part (SESSION1) → `@UriPath` field on endpoint\n- Query params → `@UriParam` fields on configuration\n\n### Annotations\n- `@Component(\"name\")` → Component discovery and scheme registration\n- `@UriEndpoint(scheme=..., syntax=..., category=...)` → Endpoint metadata\n- `@UriPath` → URI path parameter (required, part of syntax)\n- `@UriParam` → URI query parameter (configurable via ?key=value)\n- `@Metadata(required=true, description=...)` → Documentation\n\n### Configuration Flow\n1. Component receives: `fix:SESSION1?opt1=val1&opt2=val2`\n2. createEndpoint(): remaining=\"SESSION1\", parameters={opt1: val1, opt2: val2}\n3. setProperties(endpoint, parameters) → injects values via reflection/setters\n4. Endpoint configuration overrides component defaults\n\n### Async Producer Pattern\n```java\n@Override\npublic boolean process(Exchange exchange, AsyncCallback callback) {\n    try {\n        // Do async work...\n        doWork();\n        callback.done(true);\n        return true; // or false if work was deferred\n    } catch (Exception e) {\n        exchange.setException(e);\n        callback.done(false);\n        return false;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### Message Listener Pattern\n```java\n// In Consumer.doStart():\nengine.addMessageListener(sessionId, this);\n\n// Implement interface:\n@Override\npublic void onMessage(String message) {\n    Exchange exchange = createExchange();\n    exchange.getIn().setBody(message);\n    getProcessor().process(exchange);\n}\n```\n\n### POM Structure\n- Parent: `<parent>components</parent>` (inherited from components/pom.xml)\n- Dependencies: `camel-support`, plus protocol libraries\n- Test: `camel-test-spring-junit5`\n- Service descriptor: `META-INF/services/org/apache/camel/component/{name}`\n\n### Service Discovery\nFile: `src/main/resources/META-INF/services/org/apache/camel/component/fix`\nContent: `class=org.apache.camel.component.fix.FixComponent`\n\n## FIX Component Implementation Details\n\n### Custom Interfaces\n- **FixEngine**: Abstraction for FIX protocol implementation (pluggable)\n- **FixMessageListener**: Callback interface for receiving messages from engine\n\n### Configuration Fields\n- configFile (required) - FIX configuration file path\n- senderCompID - Identifier of the sender\n- targetCompID - Identifier of the target\n- fixVersion - FIX protocol version (default: FIX.4.4)\n- heartBeatInterval - Heartbeat interval in seconds (default: 30)\n- socketConnectHost - Connection host\n- socketConnectPort - Connection port (default: 9898)\n\n### Headers\n- CamelFixMessageType - Message type\n- CamelFixSessionID - Session identifier\n- CamelFixSenderCompID - Sender CompID\n- CamelFixTargetCompID - Target CompID\n\n## Camel References\n- Kafka Component: Complex async producer with configuration\n- Timer Component: Simple consumer with lifecycle management\n- Mock Component: Simple endpoint with advanced assertions\n- QuickFIX: Existing Camel FIX component for reference\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":8,"cache_creation_input_tokens":4321,"cache_read_input_tokens":95438,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":4321},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"d6b6a617-6670-4720-bf84-0de355918432","uuid":"914cb3c3-b089-42bf-832d-b77570d1e0dd"}
